	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">United States</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikiquote</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p><small>"America", "US", "USA", and "United States of America" redirect here. For the landmass comprising North, Central, South America, and the Caribbean, see <a href="/wiki/Americas" title="Americas">Americas</a>. For other uses, see <a href="/wiki/America_(disambiguation)" class="mw-disambig" title="America (disambiguation)">America (disambiguation)</a>.</small> 
</p>
<table align="center" class="NPOV" style="background: AntiqueWhite; border: 1px solid #aaa; padding: .2em; margin-bottom: 3px; font-size: 95%; width: auto;">

</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Great_Seal_of_the_United_States_(obverse).svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Great_Seal_of_the_United_States_%28obverse%29.svg/220px-Great_Seal_of_the_United_States_%28obverse%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Great_Seal_of_the_United_States_%28obverse%29.svg/330px-Great_Seal_of_the_United_States_%28obverse%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Great_Seal_of_the_United_States_%28obverse%29.svg/440px-Great_Seal_of_the_United_States_%28obverse%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Great_Seal_of_the_United_States_(obverse).svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><center><i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/E_Pluribus_Unum" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:E Pluribus Unum">E Pluribus Unum</a></i></center></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:USA123.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/USA123.jpg/220px-USA123.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/USA123.jpg/330px-USA123.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/USA123.jpg/440px-USA123.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="768" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:USA123.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The barriers of time and space vanish. All <a href="/wiki/America" class="mw-redirect" title="America">America</a> that ever was and ever will be <a href="/wiki/Lives" class="mw-redirect" title="Lives">lives</a> every <a href="/wiki/Moment" title="Moment">moment</a>. ~ <a href="/wiki/Richard_McKenna" title="Richard McKenna">Richard McKenna</a></div></div></div>
<p>The <b><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">United States of America</a></b> (<b>U.S.</b>), commonly referred to as the <b>United States</b> or <b>America</b>, is a <a href="/wiki/Countries" title="Countries">country</a> located on the continent of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_America" class="extiw" title="w:North America">North America</a>, with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Territories_of_the_United_States" class="extiw" title="w:Territories of the United States">territories</a> located on islands in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carribean_Sea" class="extiw" title="w:Carribean Sea">Carribean Sea</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" class="extiw" title="w:Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a>.&#160;The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Constitution" title="United States Constitution">Constitution of the United States</a> is the supreme law of the country.&#160;<a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a> is the most populous city in the country, whereas <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> is the most populous constituent state. The country's capital is <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a>, which is located on the northern border of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/U.S._state" class="extiw" title="w:U.S. state">U.S. state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">Virginia</a>. The United States is one of the founders of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> organization, of which it is a permanent member. The United States is the third largest country in the world by both population and land area.
</p>
<div role="navigation" style="margin-left: 2em;">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="A">A</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: A">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_22nd_Regiment,_United_States_Colored_Troops.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Flag_of_the_22nd_Regiment%2C_United_States_Colored_Troops.png/220px-Flag_of_the_22nd_Regiment%2C_United_States_Colored_Troops.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="230" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/67/Flag_of_the_22nd_Regiment%2C_United_States_Colored_Troops.png 1.5x" data-file-width="271" data-file-height="283" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_22nd_Regiment,_United_States_Colored_Troops.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Every measure of prudence, therefore, ought to be assumed for the eventual total extirpation of slavery from the United States. ~ <a href="/wiki/John_Adams" title="John Adams">John Adams</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_060421-N-3855M-001_Aviation_Machinist_Mate_3rd_Class_Mony_R._En_raises_her_right_hand_at_the_Naturalization_Ceremony_held_at_the_U._S._District_Court_Middle_Florida.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/US_Navy_060421-N-3855M-001_Aviation_Machinist_Mate_3rd_Class_Mony_R._En_raises_her_right_hand_at_the_Naturalization_Ceremony_held_at_the_U._S._District_Court_Middle_Florida.jpg/220px-thumbnail.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/US_Navy_060421-N-3855M-001_Aviation_Machinist_Mate_3rd_Class_Mony_R._En_raises_her_right_hand_at_the_Naturalization_Ceremony_held_at_the_U._S._District_Court_Middle_Florida.jpg/330px-thumbnail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/US_Navy_060421-N-3855M-001_Aviation_Machinist_Mate_3rd_Class_Mony_R._En_raises_her_right_hand_at_the_Naturalization_Ceremony_held_at_the_U._S._District_Court_Middle_Florida.jpg/440px-thumbnail.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2100" data-file-height="1500" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_060421-N-3855M-001_Aviation_Machinist_Mate_3rd_Class_Mony_R._En_raises_her_right_hand_at_the_Naturalization_Ceremony_held_at_the_U._S._District_Court_Middle_Florida.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>I have not one drop of blood in my veins but what is American. ~ <a href="/wiki/John_Adams" title="John Adams">John Adams</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bombardment_of_Fort_Sumter(3b52027r).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Bombardment_of_Fort_Sumter%283b52027r%29.jpg/220px-Bombardment_of_Fort_Sumter%283b52027r%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="160" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Bombardment_of_Fort_Sumter%283b52027r%29.jpg/330px-Bombardment_of_Fort_Sumter%283b52027r%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Bombardment_of_Fort_Sumter%283b52027r%29.jpg/440px-Bombardment_of_Fort_Sumter%283b52027r%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="466" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bombardment_of_Fort_Sumter(3b52027r).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>I shudder when I think of the calamities which slavery is likely to produce in this country. ~ <a href="/wiki/John_Adams" title="John Adams">John Adams</a></div></div></div>
<ul><li>The tank, the B-52, the fighter-bomber, the state-controlled police and military are the weapons of dictatorship. The rifle is the weapon of <a href="/wiki/Democracy" title="Democracy">democracy</a>. Not for nothing was the revolver called an 'equalizer'. <i>Egalité</i> implies <i>libertė</i>. And always will. Let us hope our weapons are never needed — but do not forget what the common people of this nation knew when they demanded the Bill of Rights: An armed citizenry is the first defense, the best defense, and the final defense against tyranny.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Edward_Abbey" title="Edward Abbey">Edward Abbey</a>, as quoted in <i>Abbey's Road</i> (1979)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Without <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Jefferson" title="Thomas Jefferson">Jefferson</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">the new nation</a> might have lost its soul. Without <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Hamilton" title="Alexander Hamilton">Hamilton</a> it would assuredly have been killed in body.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Truslow_Adams" class="extiw" title="w:James Truslow Adams">James Truslow Adams</a>, as quoted in <i>Jeffersonian Principles and Hamiltonian Principles</i> (1932), p. xvii</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>We are in the very midst of a Revolution, the most compleat, unexpected, and remarkable of any in the History of Nations.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/John_Adams" title="John Adams">John Adams</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.masshist.org/publications/apde2/view?id=ADMS-06-04-02-0109">letter to William Cushing</a> (June 9, 1776)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" class="mw-redirect" title="Great Britain">Britain</a> has been moving earth and hell to obtain allies against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">us</a>, yet it is improper in us to propose an alliance! <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" class="mw-redirect" title="Great Britain">Great Britain</a> has borrowed all the superfluous wealth of <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a>, in Italy, Germany, Holland, Switzerland, and some in France, to murder us, yet it is dishonorable in us to propose to borrow money! By heaven, I would make a bargain with all Europe, if it lay with me. Let all Europe stand still, neither lend men nor money nor ships to England nor America, and let them fight it out alone. I would give my share of millions for such a bargain. America is treated unfairly and ungenerously by <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a>. But thus it is, mankind will be servile to tyrannical masters, and basely devoted to vile idols.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/John_Adams" title="John Adams">John Adams</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oll.libertyfund.org/titles/2105#lf1431-07_head_273">letter to B. Franklin</a> (April 16, 1781), Leyden</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Neither my father or mother, grandfather or grandmother, great grandfather or great grandmother, nor any other relation that I know of, or care a farthing for, has been in <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a> these one hundred and fifty years; so that you see I have not one drop of blood in my veins but what is American.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/John_Adams" title="John Adams">John Adams</a>, to a foreign ambassador (1785), as quoted in <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=lWcsAAAAIAAJ&amp;pg=PA392">The Works of John Adams, Second President of the United States: Autobiography</a></i> (1851), by Charles F. Adams, p. 392.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Every measure of prudence, therefore, ought to be assumed for the eventual total extirpation of <a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">slavery</a> from the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">United States</a>.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/John_Adams" title="John Adams">John Adams</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oll.libertyfund.org/titles/2127#lf1431-10_head_152">letter to Robert J. Evans</a> (June 8, 1819)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>I shudder when I think of the calamities which slavery is likely to produce in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">this country</a>. You would think me mad if I were to describe my anticipations.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/John_Adams" title="John Adams">John Adams</a> (1820), as quoted in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20111029143754/http://home.nas.com/lopresti/ps2.htm"><i>John Adams</i></a> (1962), by Page Smith, Garden City, New York: Doubleday, p. 138.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Slavery in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">this country</a>, I have seen hanging over it like a black cloud for half a century.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/John_Adams" title="John Adams">John Adams</a> (1821), as quoted in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20111029143754/http://home.nas.com/lopresti/ps2.htm"><i>Passionate Sage</i></a> (1993), Joseph J. Ellis, New York: Norton, p. 138.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>America, in the assembly of nations, since her admission among them, has invariably, though often fruitlessly, held forth to them the hand of honest friendship, of equal freedom, of generous reciprocity. She has uniformly spoken among them, though often to heedless and often to disdainful ears, the language of equal liberty, of equal justice, and of equal rights. She has, in the lapse of nearly half a century, without a single exception, respected the independence of other nations while asserting and maintaining her own. She has abstained from interference in the concerns of others, even when conflict has been for principles to which she clings, as to the last vital drop that visits the heart. She has seen that probably for centuries to come, all the contests of that <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aceldama" class="extiw" title="w:Aceldama">Aceldama</a> the European world, will be contests of inveterate power, and emerging right. Wherever the standard of freedom and Independence has been or shall be unfurled, there will her heart, her benedictions and her prayers be. But she goes not abroad, in search of monsters to destroy. She is the well-wisher to the freedom and independence of all. She is the champion and vindicator only of her own. She will commend the general cause by the countenance of her voice, and the benignant sympathy of her example. She well knows that by once enlisting under other banners than her own, were they even the banners of foreign independence, she would involve herself beyond the power of extrication, in all the wars of interest and intrigue, of individual avarice, envy, and ambition, which assume the colors and usurp the standard of freedom. The fundamental maxims of her policy would insensibly change from liberty to force. The frontlet on her brows would no longer beam with the ineffable splendor of freedom and independence; but in its stead would soon be substituted an imperial diadem, flashing in false and tarnished lustre the murky radiance of dominion and power. She might become the dictatress of the world; she would be no longer the ruler of her own spirit. . . . Her glory is not dominion, but liberty. Her march is the march of the mind. She has a spear and a shield: but the motto upon her shield is, Freedom, Independence, Peace. This has been her Declaration: this has been, as far as her necessary intercourse with the rest of mankind would permit, her practice.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/John_Quincy_Adams" title="John Quincy Adams">John Quincy Adams</a>, address as Secretary of State to the U.S. House of Representatives (July 4, 1821)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>If I have a wish dearer to my soul than that my ashes may be mingled with those of a Warren and a Montgomery, it is that these American States may never cease to be free and independent.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Samuel_Adams" title="Samuel Adams">Samuel Adams</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.samuel-adams-heritage.com/documents/speech-about-declaration-of-independence.html">speech about the Declaration of Independence</a> (August 1, 1776)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>And that the said Constitution be never construed to authorize Congress to infringe the just liberty of the press, or the rights of conscience; or to prevent the people of the United States, who are peaceable citizens, from keeping their own arms.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Samuel_Adams" title="Samuel Adams">Samuel Adams</a>, (February 6, 1788), reported in Charles Hale, <i>Debates and Proceedings in the Convention of the Commonwealth of Massachusetts</i> (1856), p. 86. This language was proposed in the Massachusetts convention for ratification of the U.S. Constitution to be added to Article I of that document.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Americans have a tendency to talk about the ethos of the community, and not of the individual. You think <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2006_Lebanon_War" class="extiw" title="w:2006 Lebanon War">this war</a> is between Israel and Lebanon, for example. You think about who is right and wrong, but you don't think about the experience of the soldier.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danny_Admasu" class="extiw" title="w:Danny Admasu">Danny Admasu</a>, as quoted in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=vnnGAgAAQBAJ&amp;printsec=frontcover"><i>Searching for Zion, The Quest for Home in the African Diaspora</i></a> (2013), by Emily Raboteau, Atlantic Monthly Press, p. 45.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>In America I was liberated from a certain naïve belief in culture and attained the capacity to see culture from the outside. To clarify the point: in spite of all social criticism and all consciousness of the primacy of economic factors, the fundamental importance of the mind—“<i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Geist" class="extiw" title="w:Geist">Geist</a></i>”—was quasi a dogma self-evident to me from the very beginning. The fact that this was not a foregone conclusion, I learned in America, where no reverential silence in the presence of everything intellectual prevailed.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Theodor_Adorno" title="Theodor Adorno">Theodor Adorno</a>, as quoted in <i>The Origin of Negative Dialectics</i> (Free Press: 1977), p. 187.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>In the United States today, we have more than our share of the nattering nabobs of negativism.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Spiro_Agnew" title="Spiro Agnew">Spiro Agnew</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldaffairsjournal.org/blog/alexander-j-motyl/negativists-are-wrong-ukraine">speech in San Diego</a> (September 11, 1970)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>I'm happy. America is the country of freedom and democracy, there are jobs opportunities, there is good education, and we are looking forward to having a good life over there.
<ul><li>Ahmad al-Abboud, as quoted in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/storyline/syrias-suffering-families/first-syrian-family-surge-resettlement-program-departs-kansas-city-n551876"><i>The Associated Press</i></a> (April 6, 2016)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>I did more for the <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> serf in giving him land as well as personal liberty, than <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">America</a> did for the negro slave set free by the proclamation of <a href="/wiki/Abraham_Lincoln" title="Abraham Lincoln">President Lincoln</a>. I am at a loss to understand how you <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">Americans</a> could have been so blind as to leave the negro slave without tools to work out his salvation. In giving him personal liberty, you have him an obligation to perform to the state which he must be unable to fulfill. Without property of any kind he cannot educate himself and his children. I believe the time must come when many will question the manner of American emancipation of the negro slaves in 1863. The vote, in the hands of an ignorant man, without either property or self respect, will be used to the damage of the people at large; for the rich man, without honor or any kind of patriotism, will purchase it, and with it swamp the rights of a free people.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Alexander_II_of_Russia" title="Alexander II of Russia">Alexander II</a>, emperor of Russia, conversation with Wharton Barker, Pavlovski Palace (August 17, 1879); reported in Barker, "The Secret of Russia's Friendship", <i>The Independent</i> (March 24, 1904), p. 647.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>To make America the greatest is my goal, <br /> So I beat the Russians, and I beat the Pole, <br /> and for the USA won the medal of gold. <br /> Italians said: 'You're Greater than the Cassius of old'. <br /> We like your name, we like your game, <br /> So make Rome your home if you will. <br /> I said I appreciate your kind hospitality, <br /> But the USA is my country still, <br /> 'Cause they're waiting to welcome me in Louisville.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Muhammad_Ali" title="Muhammad Ali">Muhammad Ali</a>, poem written after winning the gold medal in the 1960 Olympic Summer Games in Rome, Italy, p. 35.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>I am America; I am the part you won't recognize. But, get used to me.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Muhammad_Ali" title="Muhammad Ali">Muhammad Ali</a>, as quoted in <i>The Greatest</i>.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Throughout the world, on any given day, a man, woman or child is likely to be displaced, tortured, killed or "disappeared", at the hands of governments or armed political groups. More often than not, the United States shares the blame.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amnesty_International" class="extiw" title="w:Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a>, 1996 Report on U. S. Military Aid and Human Rights</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>'Race' and 'ethnicity' categories have changed significantly over time to reflect changes in the American population. Since 1900, 26 different racial terms have been used to identify populations in the U.S. Census. Preserving outdated terms for the sake of questionable continuity is a disservice to the nation and the American people.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Anthropological_Association" class="extiw" title="w:American Anthropological Association">American Anthropological Association</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.aaanet.org/gvt/ombdraft.htm">"Response to OMB Directive 15"</a> (September 1997), <i>Race and Ethnic Standards for Federal Statistics and Administrative Reporting</i>, Arlington County, Virginia: American Anthropological Association.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Yet the concept of race has become thoroughly, and perniciously, woven into the cultural and political fabric of the United States. It has become an essential element of both individual identity and government policy. Because so much harm has been based on 'racial' distinctions over the years, correctives for such harm must also acknowledge the impact of 'racial' consciousness among the U.S. populace, regardless of the fact that 'race' has no scientific justification in human biology. Eventually, however, these classifications must be transcended and replaced by more non-racist and accurate ways of representing the diversity of the U.S. population. This is the dilemma and opportunity of the moment. It is important to recognize the categories to which individuals have been assigned historically in order to be vigilant about the elimination of discrimination. Yet ultimately, the effective elimination of discrimination will require an end to such categorization, and a transition toward social and cultural categories that will prove more scientifically useful and personally resonant for the public than are categories of 'race'. Redress of the past and transition for the future can be simultaneously effected.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Anthropological_Association" class="extiw" title="w:American Anthropological Association">American Anthropological Association</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.aaanet.org/gvt/ombdraft.htm">"Response to OMB Directive 15"</a> (September 1997), <i>Race and Ethnic Standards for Federal Statistics and Administrative Reporting</i>, Arlington County, Virginia: American Anthropological Association.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Negroes are American citizens. First class taxpayers, but so often treated as second class citizens, if there is such. In our hearts, we would like to know what it is that the white man has against the negro. What can we do to make peace with the white man? We have to live on this earth together. We cannot do without each other. We as a group, want your friendship, won't you accept?
<ul><li>Floy J. Anderson, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.eisenhower.archives.gov/research/online_documents/civil_rights_citizens_letters/1957_10_15_anderson.pdf">letter to Dwight Eisenhower</a> (October 15, 1957), San Francisco, California.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>The idea of America from the beginning was that you could come here, reinvent yourself, be anybody you want, live any way you wanted, believe anything you wanted. For the first few hundred years, like everywhere else in the world, celebrity and fame were a result of some kind of accomplishment or achievement, sometimes not a great accomplishment or achievement, but you did something in the world to earn renown. America really was the key place that invented the modern celebrity culture, which was, beginning a century ago, more and more not necessarily about having won a war or led a people or written a great book or painted a great painting, but about being famous, fame for its own sake. We created that, [...] certainly in the last few decades, more than ever [...] fame itself, however you've got it, was a primary goal for people.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kurt_Andersen" class="extiw" title="w:Kurt Andersen">Kurt Andersen</a> in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XirnEfkdQJM">How America Got Divorced from Reality: Christian Utopias, Anti-Elitism, Media Circus</a> (2:29), Big Think, YouTube video ( October 8, 2017)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>The better to secure and perpetuate mutual friendship and intercourse among the people of the different States in this Union, the free inhabitants of each of these States, paupers, vagabonds, and fugitives from justice excepted, shall be entitled to all privileges and immunities of free citizens in the several States...
<ul><li>Article IV, <a href="/wiki/Articles_of_Confederation" title="Articles of Confederation"><i>Articles of Confederation and Perpetual Union</i></a>.</li></ul></li></ul>

<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:North_America_satellite.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/North_America_satellite.jpg/220px-North_America_satellite.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/North_America_satellite.jpg/330px-North_America_satellite.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/North_America_satellite.jpg/440px-North_America_satellite.jpg 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="900" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:North_America_satellite.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The gem of the ocean; the home of the brave and the free. <ul><li>The power of the United States depended heavily on its pale empire of ideas, attitudes and innovations. Its ideas alighted effortlessly on foreign ground, irrespective of who owned the ground. Much of its influence came from such innovations as the telephone, electricity, aircraft and the cheap car, nuclear weapons and spacecraft, computers and the Internet. Its influence came through jazz, cartoons, Hollywood, television and popular culture. Its influence came from an excitement about technology and economic change, and a belief in incentives and individual enterprise. It was also the most ardent missionary for the creed of democracy. While military and economic might was vital to the success of the United States, the power of its pale empire of ideas was probably even more pervasive.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Geoffrey_Blainey" title="Geoffrey Blainey">Geoffrey Blainey</a>, <i>A Short History of the World</i> (2000).</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>The global role of the United States is perhaps the ultimate chapter in that long period of European expansion which had begun in western Europe, and especially on the Atlantic seaboard, during the 15th century. Europe slowly had outgrown its homeland. Its cultural empire eventually formed a long band traversing most of the Northern Hemisphere and dipping far into the Southern. The modern hub of the peoples and ideas of European origin is now New York as much as Paris, or Los Angeles as much as London. In the history of the European peoples the city of Washington is perhaps what Constantinople - the infant city of Emperor Constantine - was to the last phase of the Roman Empire; for it is unlikely that Europeans, a century hence, will continue to stamp the world so decisively with their ideas and inventions.

<ul><li>A 'superpower' is a country that wields enough military, political and economic might to convince nations in all parts of the world to do things they otherwise wouldn't. China's headline growth may be higher, but it's the U.S. economy that's allowing its citizens to grow along with it... America's military superiority remains unrivaled; full stop...</p><p>The U.S. dominates across land, sea, air and space. America's Middle East misadventures gave the U.S. military a black eye, but the wars in Iraq and Afghanistan speak more to the changing nature of warfare than declining U.S. military superiority. Terrorists and guerrilla fighters give conventional military powers fits by design. The U.S. must ultimately learn to scale down to better meet those challenges. Nevertheless, while conventional military strength might not deter terrorists, it still does a terrific job of deterring hostile nations...</p><p>In order to have political power abroad, you must first have stability at home. The U.S. has the oldest working national constitution in the world, as well as strong institutions and rule of law to accompany it. While far from perfect, the governing document created by America’s founding fathers has evolved along with its people. The numbers show the enduring attraction of this system: 45 million people living in the U.S. today were born in a foreign country. That is more than four times higher than the next highest country. <ul><li>The USA is the world's foremost economic and military power, with global interests and an unmatched global reach. <ul><li>Our identity as a nation — unlike many other nations — is not determined by geography or ethnicity, by soil or blood. Being an American involves the embrace of high ideals and civic responsibility. We become the heirs of Thomas Jefferson by accepting the ideal of human dignity found in the Declaration of Independence. We become the heirs of James Madison by understanding the genius and values of the U.S. Constitution. We become the heirs of Martin Luther King, Jr., by recognizing one another not by the color of their skin, but by the content of their character. This means that people of every race, religion, and ethnicity can be fully and equally American. It means that bigotry or white supremacy in any form is blasphemy against the American creed. And it means that the very identity of our nation depends on the passing of civic ideals to the next generation... Self-correction is the secret strength of freedom. We are a nation with a history of resilience and a genius for renewal.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=S2YlVZxu_L0">remarks at Bush Institute Summit, "The Spirit of Liberty: At Home, In The World" at the Bush Institute Summit in New York City</a> (October 2017), as quoted in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://archive.is/jl9AF#selection-2115.0-2135.112"><i>The Washington Post</i></a> (October 2017)</li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="C">C</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: C">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:McDonald%27s,_Germantown,_Maryland,_September_9,_2013.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/McDonald%27s%2C_Germantown%2C_Maryland%2C_September_9%2C_2013.JPG/220px-McDonald%27s%2C_Germantown%2C_Maryland%2C_September_9%2C_2013.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/McDonald%27s%2C_Germantown%2C_Maryland%2C_September_9%2C_2013.JPG/330px-McDonald%27s%2C_Germantown%2C_Maryland%2C_September_9%2C_2013.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/McDonald%27s%2C_Germantown%2C_Maryland%2C_September_9%2C_2013.JPG/440px-McDonald%27s%2C_Germantown%2C_Maryland%2C_September_9%2C_2013.JPG 2x" data-file-width="3680" data-file-height="2760" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:McDonald%27s,_Germantown,_Maryland,_September_9,_2013.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Americans love to eat. They are fatally attracted to the slow death of fast food. ~ <a href="/wiki/George_Carlin" title="George Carlin">George Carlin</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Stokely_Carmichael_in_Alabama_1966.jpeg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Stokely_Carmichael_in_Alabama_1966.jpeg/220px-Stokely_Carmichael_in_Alabama_1966.jpeg" decoding="async" width="220" height="294" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/1a/Stokely_Carmichael_in_Alabama_1966.jpeg 1.5x" data-file-width="290" data-file-height="387" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Stokely_Carmichael_in_Alabama_1966.jpeg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>For a century, this nation has been like an octopus of exploitation, its tentacles stretching from Mississippi and Harlem to South America, the Middle East, southern Africa, and Vietnam; the form of exploitation varies from area to area but the essential result has been the same—a powerful few have been maintained and enriched at the expense of the poor and voiceless colored masses. This pattern must be broken. ~ <a href="/wiki/Stokely_Carmichael" title="Stokely Carmichael">Stokely Carmichael</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Jimmy_Carter.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Jimmy_Carter.jpg/220px-Jimmy_Carter.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="326" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Jimmy_Carter.jpg/330px-Jimmy_Carter.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Jimmy_Carter.jpg/440px-Jimmy_Carter.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2777" data-file-height="4109" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Jimmy_Carter.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>We've become now an <a href="/wiki/Oligarchy" title="Oligarchy">oligarchy</a> instead of a democracy. And I think that's been the worst damage to the basic moral and ethical standards of the American political system that I've ever seen in my life. ~ <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Carter" title="Jimmy Carter">Jimmy Carter</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Capitol_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Capitol_2.jpg/220px-Capitol_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="145" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Capitol_2.jpg/330px-Capitol_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Capitol_2.jpg/440px-Capitol_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="700" data-file-height="460" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Capitol_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>We have built no national temples but the Capitol; we consult no common oracle but the Constitution. ~ <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Choate" title="Rufus Choate">Rufus Choate</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ward_Churchill.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Ward_Churchill.jpg/220px-Ward_Churchill.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="293" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Ward_Churchill.jpg/330px-Ward_Churchill.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Ward_Churchill.jpg/440px-Ward_Churchill.jpg 2x" data-file-width="533" data-file-height="711" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ward_Churchill.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>I hear Republicans and Libertarians and so forth talking about property rights, but they stop talking about property rights as soon as the subject of American Indians comes up, because they know fully well, perhaps not in a fully articulated, conscious form, but they know fully well that the basis for the very system of endeavor and enterprise and profitability to which they are committed and devoted accrues on the basis of theft of the resources of someone else. They are in possession of stolen property. They know it. They all know it. It's a dishonest endeavor from day one. ~ <a href="/wiki/Ward_Churchill" title="Ward Churchill">Ward Churchill</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Capitol_west_side.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/US_Capitol_west_side.JPG/220px-US_Capitol_west_side.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="114" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/US_Capitol_west_side.JPG/330px-US_Capitol_west_side.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/US_Capitol_west_side.JPG/440px-US_Capitol_west_side.JPG 2x" data-file-width="3865" data-file-height="2000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Capitol_west_side.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Our democracy must be not only the envy of the world but the engine of our own renewal. ~ <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lyndon_Johnson_and_Martin_Luther_King,_Jr._-_Voting_Rights_Act.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Lyndon_Johnson_and_Martin_Luther_King%2C_Jr._-_Voting_Rights_Act.jpg/220px-Lyndon_Johnson_and_Martin_Luther_King%2C_Jr._-_Voting_Rights_Act.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Lyndon_Johnson_and_Martin_Luther_King%2C_Jr._-_Voting_Rights_Act.jpg/330px-Lyndon_Johnson_and_Martin_Luther_King%2C_Jr._-_Voting_Rights_Act.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Lyndon_Johnson_and_Martin_Luther_King%2C_Jr._-_Voting_Rights_Act.jpg/440px-Lyndon_Johnson_and_Martin_Luther_King%2C_Jr._-_Voting_Rights_Act.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3000" data-file-height="2009" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Lyndon_Johnson_and_Martin_Luther_King,_Jr._-_Voting_Rights_Act.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>There is nothing wrong with America that cannot be cured by what is right with America. ~ <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Borderwallbrownsvile.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Borderwallbrownsvile.jpg/200px-Borderwallbrownsvile.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="267" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Borderwallbrownsvile.jpg/300px-Borderwallbrownsvile.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Borderwallbrownsvile.jpg/400px-Borderwallbrownsvile.jpg 2x" data-file-width="768" data-file-height="1024" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Borderwallbrownsvile.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>And throughout the history of the borderlands, the <a href="/wiki/Military" title="Military">military</a> or armed <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/militias" class="extiw" title="w:militias">militias</a> have been dispatched there to keep <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Black_people" class="extiw" title="w:Black people">black</a> <a href="/wiki/Slaves" class="mw-redirect" title="Slaves">slaves</a> from fleeing, remove <a href="/w/index.php?title=Native_Americans&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Native Americans (page does not exist)">Native Americans</a> from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancestral_lands" class="extiw" title="w:Ancestral lands">ancestral lands</a> and suppress <a href="/wiki/Mexican" class="mw-redirect" title="Mexican">Mexican</a>-<a href="/wiki/American" class="mw-redirect" title="American">American</a> revolts stemming from <a href="/wiki/Anger" title="Anger">anger</a> over white mob <a href="/wiki/Violence" title="Violence">violence</a>. ~ Russell Contreras</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Greater_coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Greater_coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg/220px-Greater_coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="232" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Greater_coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg/330px-Greater_coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Greater_coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg/440px-Greater_coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="451" data-file-height="476" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Greater_coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>America at least has demonstrated that republics are not ungrateful. It is one of the glories of our country that so long as we remain faithful to the cause of justice and truth and liberty, this action will continue. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:1807_half_dollar_rev.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/1807_half_dollar_rev.jpg/220px-1807_half_dollar_rev.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/1c/1807_half_dollar_rev.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="300" data-file-height="300" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:1807_half_dollar_rev.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>We've gotten to where we've nearly 'them'ed ourselves to death. <div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_United_States_(1777-1795).svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg/220px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="116" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg/330px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg/440px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281777-1795%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="2470" data-file-height="1300" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_United_States_(1777-1795).svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>When the people of the colonies were defending their liberties against the might of kings, they chose their banner from the design set in the firmament through all eternity. The flags of great empires of that day have gone, but the stars and stripes remain. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_030501-N-8029P-003_A_total_of_43_sailors_assigned_to_USS_Abraham_Lincoln_(CVN_72)_take_the_oath_of_citizenship_upon_the_completion_of_a_naturalization_ceremony.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/US_Navy_030501-N-8029P-003_A_total_of_43_sailors_assigned_to_USS_Abraham_Lincoln_%28CVN_72%29_take_the_oath_of_citizenship_upon_the_completion_of_a_naturalization_ceremony.jpg/220px-thumbnail.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/US_Navy_030501-N-8029P-003_A_total_of_43_sailors_assigned_to_USS_Abraham_Lincoln_%28CVN_72%29_take_the_oath_of_citizenship_upon_the_completion_of_a_naturalization_ceremony.jpg/330px-thumbnail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/US_Navy_030501-N-8029P-003_A_total_of_43_sailors_assigned_to_USS_Abraham_Lincoln_%28CVN_72%29_take_the_oath_of_citizenship_upon_the_completion_of_a_naturalization_ceremony.jpg/440px-thumbnail.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2100" data-file-height="1500" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_030501-N-8029P-003_A_total_of_43_sailors_assigned_to_USS_Abraham_Lincoln_(CVN_72)_take_the_oath_of_citizenship_upon_the_completion_of_a_naturalization_ceremony.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>America is a large country. <div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_090918-N-2013O-142_Service_members_and_family_members_recite_the_oath_of_allegiance_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_at_Commander,_Fleet_Activities_Yokosuka.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/US_Navy_090918-N-2013O-142_Service_members_and_family_members_recite_the_oath_of_allegiance_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_at_Commander%2C_Fleet_Activities_Yokosuka.jpg/220px-thumbnail.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/US_Navy_090918-N-2013O-142_Service_members_and_family_members_recite_the_oath_of_allegiance_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_at_Commander%2C_Fleet_Activities_Yokosuka.jpg/330px-thumbnail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/US_Navy_090918-N-2013O-142_Service_members_and_family_members_recite_the_oath_of_allegiance_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_at_Commander%2C_Fleet_Activities_Yokosuka.jpg/440px-thumbnail.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2100" data-file-height="1500" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_090918-N-2013O-142_Service_members_and_family_members_recite_the_oath_of_allegiance_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_at_Commander,_Fleet_Activities_Yokosuka.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>There is no better American spirit than that which is exhibited by many of those who have recently come to our shores. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_100804-N-6770T-031_Sailors,_Airmen,_and_Soldiers_from_nations_around_the_world_swear_in_as_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_USS_Port_Royal_(CG_73).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/US_Navy_100804-N-6770T-031_Sailors%2C_Airmen%2C_and_Soldiers_from_nations_around_the_world_swear_in_as_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_USS_Port_Royal_%28CG_73%29.jpg/220px-thumbnail.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/US_Navy_100804-N-6770T-031_Sailors%2C_Airmen%2C_and_Soldiers_from_nations_around_the_world_swear_in_as_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_USS_Port_Royal_%28CG_73%29.jpg/330px-thumbnail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/US_Navy_100804-N-6770T-031_Sailors%2C_Airmen%2C_and_Soldiers_from_nations_around_the_world_swear_in_as_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_USS_Port_Royal_%28CG_73%29.jpg/440px-thumbnail.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2136" data-file-height="1526" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_100804-N-6770T-031_Sailors,_Airmen,_and_Soldiers_from_nations_around_the_world_swear_in_as_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_USS_Port_Royal_(CG_73).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>We are situated differently in this respect from any other country. All the other great powers have a comparatively homogeneous population, close kindred in race and blood and speech, and commonly little divided in religious beliefs. Our great nation is made up of the strong and virile pioneering stock of nearly all the countries of the world. We have a variety of race and language and religious belief. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg/220px-Coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="275" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg/330px-Coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg/440px-Coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="300" data-file-height="375" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Coat_of_arms_of_the_United_States.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>American citizenship is a high estate. He who holds it is the peer of kings. It has been secured only by untold toil and effort. It will be maintained by no other method. It demands the best that men and women have to give, but it likewise awards to its partakers the best that there is on earth. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:DA-SD-05-00599.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/DA-SD-05-00599.jpg/220px-DA-SD-05-00599.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="335" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/DA-SD-05-00599.jpg/330px-DA-SD-05-00599.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/DA-SD-05-00599.jpg/440px-DA-SD-05-00599.jpg 2x" data-file-width="887" data-file-height="1350" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:DA-SD-05-00599.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/African_American" class="extiw" title="w:African American">Colored people</a> have repeatedly proved their devotion to the high ideals of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">our country</a>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/African_American" class="extiw" title="w:African American">They</a> gave <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/African_American" class="extiw" title="w:African American">their</a> services in <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">the war</a> with the same <a href="/wiki/Patriotism" title="Patriotism">patriotism</a> and readiness that other citizens did. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_100308-N-7280V-224_Sailors_recite_the_pledge_of_allegiance_as_they_become_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_the_U.S._7th_Fleet_command_ship_USS_Blue_Ridge_(LCC_19).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/US_Navy_100308-N-7280V-224_Sailors_recite_the_pledge_of_allegiance_as_they_become_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_the_U.S._7th_Fleet_command_ship_USS_Blue_Ridge_%28LCC_19%29.jpg/220px-thumbnail.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="139" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/US_Navy_100308-N-7280V-224_Sailors_recite_the_pledge_of_allegiance_as_they_become_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_the_U.S._7th_Fleet_command_ship_USS_Blue_Ridge_%28LCC_19%29.jpg/330px-thumbnail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/US_Navy_100308-N-7280V-224_Sailors_recite_the_pledge_of_allegiance_as_they_become_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_the_U.S._7th_Fleet_command_ship_USS_Blue_Ridge_%28LCC_19%29.jpg/440px-thumbnail.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2372" data-file-height="1500" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_100308-N-7280V-224_Sailors_recite_the_pledge_of_allegiance_as_they_become_U.S._citizens_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_aboard_the_U.S._7th_Fleet_command_ship_USS_Blue_Ridge_(LCC_19).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>It is one of the anomalies of the human story that these peoples, who could not be assimilated and unified... should on coming to America discover an amazing genius for cooperation, for fusion, and for harmonious effort. Yet they were the same people when they came here that they had been on the other side... Quite apparently, they found something in our institutions, something in the American system of Government and society which they themselves helped to construct, that furnished to all of them a political and cultural common denominator. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:USMC-100201-M-4752B-003.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/USMC-100201-M-4752B-003.jpg/220px-USMC-100201-M-4752B-003.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="330" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/USMC-100201-M-4752B-003.jpg/330px-USMC-100201-M-4752B-003.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/USMC-100201-M-4752B-003.jpg/440px-USMC-100201-M-4752B-003.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2592" data-file-height="3888" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:USMC-100201-M-4752B-003.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Perhaps no country on earth has greater responsibilities than <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">America</a>. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Top_of_Rock_Cropped.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Top_of_Rock_Cropped.jpg/220px-Top_of_Rock_Cropped.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="142" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Top_of_Rock_Cropped.jpg/330px-Top_of_Rock_Cropped.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Top_of_Rock_Cropped.jpg/440px-Top_of_Rock_Cropped.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1724" data-file-height="1111" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Top_of_Rock_Cropped.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Our experience in that respect ought not to lead us too hastily to assume that we have been therefore better than other people, but certainly we have been more fortunate. We came on the stage at a later time, so that this country had presented to it, already attained, a civilization that other countries had secured only as a result of a long and painful struggle. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_100208-N-2475A-088_Sailors_stand_by_for_morning_colors_aboard_the_Nimitz-class_aircraft_carrier_USS_John_C._Stennis_(CVN_74).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/US_Navy_100208-N-2475A-088_Sailors_stand_by_for_morning_colors_aboard_the_Nimitz-class_aircraft_carrier_USS_John_C._Stennis_%28CVN_74%29.jpg/220px-US_Navy_100208-N-2475A-088_Sailors_stand_by_for_morning_colors_aboard_the_Nimitz-class_aircraft_carrier_USS_John_C._Stennis_%28CVN_74%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="116" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/US_Navy_100208-N-2475A-088_Sailors_stand_by_for_morning_colors_aboard_the_Nimitz-class_aircraft_carrier_USS_John_C._Stennis_%28CVN_74%29.jpg/330px-US_Navy_100208-N-2475A-088_Sailors_stand_by_for_morning_colors_aboard_the_Nimitz-class_aircraft_carrier_USS_John_C._Stennis_%28CVN_74%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/US_Navy_100208-N-2475A-088_Sailors_stand_by_for_morning_colors_aboard_the_Nimitz-class_aircraft_carrier_USS_John_C._Stennis_%28CVN_74%29.jpg/440px-US_Navy_100208-N-2475A-088_Sailors_stand_by_for_morning_colors_aboard_the_Nimitz-class_aircraft_carrier_USS_John_C._Stennis_%28CVN_74%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3182" data-file-height="1683" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_100208-N-2475A-088_Sailors_stand_by_for_morning_colors_aboard_the_Nimitz-class_aircraft_carrier_USS_John_C._Stennis_(CVN_74).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>We went in and came out singularly free from those questionable causes and results which have often characterized other wars. We were not moved by the age-old antagonisms of racial jealousies and hatreds. We were not seeking to gratify the ambitions of any reigning dynasty. We were not inspired by trade and commercial rivalries. We harbored no imperialistic designs. We feared no other country. We coveted no territory. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:080930-110605_-_SGT_Lisa_Morales_awaits_turn.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/080930-110605_-_SGT_Lisa_Morales_awaits_turn.jpg/220px-080930-110605_-_SGT_Lisa_Morales_awaits_turn.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/080930-110605_-_SGT_Lisa_Morales_awaits_turn.jpg/330px-080930-110605_-_SGT_Lisa_Morales_awaits_turn.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/080930-110605_-_SGT_Lisa_Morales_awaits_turn.jpg/440px-080930-110605_-_SGT_Lisa_Morales_awaits_turn.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2144" data-file-height="1424" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:080930-110605_-_SGT_Lisa_Morales_awaits_turn.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>We have waged no wars to determine a succession, establish a dynasty, or glorify a reigning house. Our military operations have been for the service of the cause of humanity. The principles on which they have been fought have more and more come to be accepted as the ultimate standards of the world. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Iraqi_child_with_U.S._Troops.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Iraqi_child_with_U.S._Troops.jpg/220px-Iraqi_child_with_U.S._Troops.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Iraqi_child_with_U.S._Troops.jpg/330px-Iraqi_child_with_U.S._Troops.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Iraqi_child_with_U.S._Troops.jpg/440px-Iraqi_child_with_U.S._Troops.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2100" data-file-height="1395" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Iraqi_child_with_U.S._Troops.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The spirit of America is to help everybody and injure nobody. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>

<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:1.12.02NewYorkStockExchangeByLuigiNovi1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/1.12.02NewYorkStockExchangeByLuigiNovi1.jpg/220px-1.12.02NewYorkStockExchangeByLuigiNovi1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/1.12.02NewYorkStockExchangeByLuigiNovi1.jpg/330px-1.12.02NewYorkStockExchangeByLuigiNovi1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/1.12.02NewYorkStockExchangeByLuigiNovi1.jpg/440px-1.12.02NewYorkStockExchangeByLuigiNovi1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="960" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:1.12.02NewYorkStockExchangeByLuigiNovi1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The chief business of the American people is business. <div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_100920-N-6632S-068_Sailors_raise_their_right_hands_while_reciting_the_oath_of_citizenship_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_in_the_hangar_ba.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/US_Navy_100920-N-6632S-068_Sailors_raise_their_right_hands_while_reciting_the_oath_of_citizenship_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_in_the_hangar_ba.jpg/220px-US_Navy_100920-N-6632S-068_Sailors_raise_their_right_hands_while_reciting_the_oath_of_citizenship_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_in_the_hangar_ba.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/US_Navy_100920-N-6632S-068_Sailors_raise_their_right_hands_while_reciting_the_oath_of_citizenship_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_in_the_hangar_ba.jpg/330px-US_Navy_100920-N-6632S-068_Sailors_raise_their_right_hands_while_reciting_the_oath_of_citizenship_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_in_the_hangar_ba.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/US_Navy_100920-N-6632S-068_Sailors_raise_their_right_hands_while_reciting_the_oath_of_citizenship_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_in_the_hangar_ba.jpg/440px-US_Navy_100920-N-6632S-068_Sailors_raise_their_right_hands_while_reciting_the_oath_of_citizenship_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_in_the_hangar_ba.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2100" data-file-height="1500" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_100920-N-6632S-068_Sailors_raise_their_right_hands_while_reciting_the_oath_of_citizenship_during_a_naturalization_ceremony_in_the_hangar_ba.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>As a nation, our first duty must be to those who are already our inhabitants, whether native or immigrants. To them we owe an especial and a weighty obligation. They came to us with stout hearts and high hopes of bettering their estate. They have contributed much to making our country what it is. They magnificently proved their loyalty by contributing their full part when the war made demand for sacrifices by all Americans. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Freedom_Day,_Claiborne_County,_Mississippi.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Freedom_Day%2C_Claiborne_County%2C_Mississippi.jpg/220px-Freedom_Day%2C_Claiborne_County%2C_Mississippi.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="181" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Freedom_Day%2C_Claiborne_County%2C_Mississippi.jpg/330px-Freedom_Day%2C_Claiborne_County%2C_Mississippi.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Freedom_Day%2C_Claiborne_County%2C_Mississippi.jpg/440px-Freedom_Day%2C_Claiborne_County%2C_Mississippi.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="657" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Freedom_Day,_Claiborne_County,_Mississippi.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>People have marveled at the growth and strength of America. They have wondered how a few weak and discordant colonies were able to win their independence from one of the greatest powers of the world. They have been amazed at our genius for self-government. They have been unable to comprehend how the shock of a great Civil War did not destroy our Union. They do not understand the economic progress of our people. It is true that we have had the advantage of great natural resources, but those have not been exclusively ours. Others have been equally fortunate in that direction. The progress of America has been due to the spirit of the people. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_United_States_(1912-1959).svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/220px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="116" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/330px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg/440px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281912-1959%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1235" data-file-height="650" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_United_States_(1912-1959).svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Alone of all flags, it expresses the sovereignty of the people which endures when all else passes away. Speaking with their voice, it has the sanctity of revelations. He who lives under it and disloyal to it is a traitor to the human race everywhere. What could be saved if the flag of the American nation were to perish? ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_men%27s_soccer_team_trains_in_NJ_2010-05-20.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/US_men%27s_soccer_team_trains_in_NJ_2010-05-20.jpg/220px-US_men%27s_soccer_team_trains_in_NJ_2010-05-20.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/US_men%27s_soccer_team_trains_in_NJ_2010-05-20.jpg/330px-US_men%27s_soccer_team_trains_in_NJ_2010-05-20.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/US_men%27s_soccer_team_trains_in_NJ_2010-05-20.jpg/440px-US_men%27s_soccer_team_trains_in_NJ_2010-05-20.jpg 2x" data-file-width="480" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_men%27s_soccer_team_trains_in_NJ_2010-05-20.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>In the case of a people which represents many nations, cultures, and races, as does our own, a unification of interests and ideals in recreations is bound to wield a telling influence for solidarity of the entire population. No more truly democratic force can be set off against the tendency to class and caste than the democracy of individual parts and prowess in sport. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:NYSE_Wall_St_2002.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/NYSE_Wall_St_2002.jpg/220px-NYSE_Wall_St_2002.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/NYSE_Wall_St_2002.jpg/330px-NYSE_Wall_St_2002.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/NYSE_Wall_St_2002.jpg/440px-NYSE_Wall_St_2002.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1544" data-file-height="1024" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:NYSE_Wall_St_2002.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Our inhabitants are especially free to promote their own welfare. They are unburdened by militarism. They are not called upon to support any imperialistic designs. Every mother can rest in the assurance that her children will find here a land of devotion, prosperity and peace. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:U.S._Capitol_Washington_D.C..jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/U.S._Capitol_Washington_D.C..jpg/220px-U.S._Capitol_Washington_D.C..jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="145" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/U.S._Capitol_Washington_D.C..jpg/330px-U.S._Capitol_Washington_D.C..jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/U.S._Capitol_Washington_D.C..jpg/440px-U.S._Capitol_Washington_D.C..jpg 2x" data-file-width="1655" data-file-height="1088" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:U.S._Capitol_Washington_D.C..jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>American government was the result of an effort to establish institutions under which the people as a whole should have the largest possible advantages. Class and privilege were outlawed, freedom and opportunity were guaranteed. They undertook to provide conditions under which service would be adequately rewarded, and where the people would own their own property and control their own government. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:GEN_Colin_Powell.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/GEN_Colin_Powell.JPG/220px-GEN_Colin_Powell.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="283" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/GEN_Colin_Powell.JPG/330px-GEN_Colin_Powell.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/GEN_Colin_Powell.JPG/440px-GEN_Colin_Powell.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2315" data-file-height="2979" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:GEN_Colin_Powell.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Bigotry" title="Bigotry">propaganda of prejudice and hatred</a> which sought to keep the colored men from supporting the national cause completely failed. The black man showed himself the same kind of citizen, moved by the same kind of <a href="/wiki/Patriotism" title="Patriotism">patriotism</a>, as the white man. They were tempted, but not one betrayed <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">his country</a>. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Henry_Johnson.PNG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Henry_Johnson.PNG/220px-Henry_Johnson.PNG" decoding="async" width="220" height="321" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Henry_Johnson.PNG/330px-Henry_Johnson.PNG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Henry_Johnson.PNG/440px-Henry_Johnson.PNG 2x" data-file-width="635" data-file-height="926" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Henry_Johnson.PNG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>During <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">the war</a> 500,000 colored men and boys were called up under the draft, not one of whom sought to evade it. They took their places wherever assigned in defense of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">the nation of which they are just as truly citizens</a> as are any others. ~ <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a></div></div></div>

<ul><li>Ultimately, the economic foundations of this country must be shaken if black people are to control their lives. The colonies of the United States—and this includes the black ghettoes within its borders, north and south—must be liberated. <ul><li>It violates the essence of what made America a great country in its political system. Now it’s just an <a href="/wiki/Oligarchy" title="Oligarchy">oligarchy</a> with unlimited political bribery being the essence of getting the nominations for president or being elected president. And the same thing applies to governors, and U.S. Senators and congress members. So, now we’ve just seen a subversion of our political system as a payoff to major contributors, who want and expect, and sometimes get, favors for themselves after the election is over... At the present time the incumbents, Democrats and Republicans, look upon this unlimited money as a great benefit to themselves. <ul><li>My estimate of American character has improved, contrary to my expectations, by this visit...I find myself in love with their intelligence, their sincerity, and the decorous self-respect that actuates all classes. They have not, ‘tis true, the force of Englishmen in personal weight or strength, but they have compensated for this deficiency by quickening the momentum of their enterprises. All is in favour of celerity of action and the saving of time. Speed, speed, speed, is the motto that is stamped in the form of their ships and steamboats, in the breed of their horses, and the light construction of their wagons and carts: and in the ten thousand contrivances that are met with here, whether for the abridging of the labour of months or minutes, whether a high-pressure engine or a patent boot-jack. All is done in pursuit of one common object, the economy of time.
