It has exercised a quite clinical manipulation of power worldwide while masquerading as a force for universal good. It’s a brilliant, even witty, highly successful act of hypnosis.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Harold_Pinter" title="Harold Pinter">Harold Pinter</a>, "Art, Truth &amp; Politics," <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://nobelprize.org/nobel_prizes/literature/laureates/2005/pinter-lecture-e.html">Nobel lecture (7 December 2005)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>I pledge allegiance to the flag of the United States of America, and to the republic for which it stands, one nation indivisible, with liberty and justice for all.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Pledge_of_Allegiance" title="Pledge of Allegiance">Pledge of Allegiance to the United States of America</a> (1923&#8211;1954)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>I pledge allegiance to the flag of the United States of America, and to the republic for which it stands, one nation under God, indivisible, with liberty and justice for all.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Pledge_of_Allegiance" title="Pledge of Allegiance">Pledge of Allegiance to the United States of America</a> (1954&#8211;present)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>I love our flag, our constitution, and our country, with a love that has no bounds. I defended all three for 35 years as a soldier and was willing to give my life in their defense. Americans revere their flag as a symbol of the nation.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Colin_Powell" title="Colin Powell">Colin Powell</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aclu.org/free-speech/letter-colin-powell">letter to Patrick Leahy</a> (18 May 1999)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Far from being the Great Satan, I would say that <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">we</a> are the Great Protector. We have sent men and women from the armed forces of the United States to other parts of the world throughout the past century to put down oppression. We defeated Fascism. We defeated Communism. We saved Europe in World War I and World War II. We were willing to do it, glad to do it. We went to Korea. We went to Vietnam. All in the interest of preserving the rights of people. And when all those conflicts were over, what did we do? Did we stay and conquer? Did we say, 'Okay, we defeated Germany. Now Germany belongs to us? We defeated Japan, so Japan belongs to us'? No. What did we do? We built them up. We gave them democratic systems which they have embraced totally to their soul. And did we ask for any land? No. The only land we ever asked for was enough land to bury our dead, and that is the kind of nation we are.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Colin_Powell" title="Colin Powell">Colin Powell</a>, as quoted in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20020220234413/http://www.cnn.com/2002/ALLPOLITICS/02/15/powell.mtv/index.html"><i>MTV Global Discussion</i></a> (14 February 2002)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Well, the correct answer is, <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">he</a> is not a Muslim, he's a Christian. He's always been a Christian. But the really right answer is, what if he is? Is there something wrong with being a Muslim in this country? The answer's no, that's not America.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Colin_Powell" title="Colin Powell">Colin Powell</a>, as quoted in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/27266223/page/2/"><i>Meet the Press</i></a> (19 October 2008)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Some anti-Americanism derives simply from our being a colossus that bestrides the earth. This resentment may be incurable. But much anti-Americanism derives from the role U.S. political, economic, and military power has played in denying such freedoms to others.  U.S. foreign policy has to be rethought. It needs not tweaking but overhauling. We need: a historical reckoning with crimes committed, sponsored, or permitted by the United States. [..] A country has to look back before it can move forward. Instituting a doctrine of the mea culpa would enhance our credibility by showing that American decision-makers do not endorse the sins of their predecessors. When <a href="/wiki/Willy_Brandt" title="Willy Brandt">Brandt</a> went down on one knee in the Warsaw ghetto [in 1970], his gesture was gratifying to World War II survivors, but it was also ennobling and cathartic for Germany. Would such an approach be futile for the United States?
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Samantha_Power" title="Samantha Power">Samantha Power</a>, article in <i>The New Republic</i>, 2003. Quoted in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424127887323844804578527181938275090.html?mod=googlenews_wsj"><i>The Wall Street Journal</i></a>.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>In America, Jews live in unprecedented equality and security, and America is Israel's defender. The reason is not just that America is so tolerant a society. America does not merely tolerate Jews and Judaism, it honors them. It does so in large part because the United States is the only country that has long defined itself as Judeo-Christian. There are Christian countries, secular countries, and Muslim countries, but America is the only Judeo-Christian country.
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=VK0llzUqQ2YC&amp;dq=%22Why+the+Jews%22&amp;source=gbs_navlinks_s"><i>Why the Jews?: The Reason for Antisemitism</i></a> (2003), by Dennis Prager and Joseph Telushkin, p. xviii</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>America-hatred has become a moral litmus test of nations, regimes, and individuals. America represents freedom, a higher quality of life, and a willingness to fight for its values. These qualities are despised by regimes characterized by tyranny and socioeconomic failure, and by individuals in the west who support such regimes or who wish to denigrate America for reasons akin to those of antisemites in their denigration of Jews. With all its flaws, America alone stands between democracy and the ascent of tyranny throughout the world.
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=VK0llzUqQ2YC&amp;dq=%22Why+the+Jews%22&amp;source=gbs_navlinks_s"><i>Why the Jews?: The Reason for Antisemitism</i></a> (2003), by Dennis Prager and Joseph Telushkin, p. 194</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>It is small surprise that among tyrannical regimes and their defenders, America and Israel are so often identified as the same enemy. This is not merely a consequence of America's standing along behind Israel; the United States has aided various Arab countries very generously, and it has on some critical occasions backed Arab regimes, such as Nasser's Egypt in 1956 and Saudi Arabia in 1981, against Israel. The hostility is aroused largely because America and Israel represent democracy, equal rights for women, a higher quality of life, and a willingness to confront despotism. That is why the two non-Muslim countries that have suffered the heaviest lossest from Islamic suicide murderers are Israel and the United States.
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=VK0llzUqQ2YC&amp;dq=%22Why+the+Jews%22&amp;source=gbs_navlinks_s"><i>Why the Jews?: The Reason for Antisemitism</i></a> (2003), by Dennis Prager and Joseph Telushkin, p. 194</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Yet despite all this hatred, America remains the dreamed-for haven of the world's oppressed; and Israel remains and embattled democracy in the midst of authoritarian states, and the birthplace of the kibbutz to which tens of thousands of youth from around the world have turned for a living lesson in human equality. America today with all its imperfections represents a model of something better, fighting for its ideals and in so doing constituting a moral challenge to others.
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=VK0llzUqQ2YC&amp;dq=%22Why+the+Jews%22&amp;source=gbs_navlinks_s"><i>Why the Jews?: The Reason for Antisemitism</i></a> (2003), by Dennis Prager and Joseph Telushkin, p. 195</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Thomas Jefferson wrote the Declaration of Independence, the document that articulated the principle of human rights endowed by the Creator, thereby ultimately ensuring the end of slavery, and led to the establishment of the country that has served as the beacon of hope for people of every race and ethnicity. More black Africans have voluntarily emigrated to the United States to seek liberty and opportunity than came to America as slaves... Conservatives view America as President Abraham Lincoln viewed it; as the 'Last Best Hope of Earth'... America gradually became the least-xenophobic, least-racist nation in the world. In no country do people become accepted as full members of the society as do immigrants to America.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Dennis_Prager" title="Dennis Prager">Dennis Prager</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.nationalreview.com/article/421681/why-left-hates-america-dennis-prager">"Why the Left Hates America"</a> (28 July 2015), <i>National Review</i></li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>Most Americans no longer know what America stands for. For them, America has become just another country, a place located between Canada and Mexico. But America was founded to be an idea, not another country.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Dennis_Prager" title="Dennis Prager">Dennis Prager</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.nationalreview.com/article/435195/donald-trump-won-because-many-republicans-arent-conservative">"The Scariest Reason Trump Won"</a> (10 May 2016), <i>National Review</i></li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>When the thirteen stripes and stars first appeared at Canton, much curiosity was excited among the people. News was circulated that a strange ship had arrived from the further end of the world, bearing a flag 'as beautiful as a flower'. Every body went to see the <i>kwa kee chuen</i>, or 'flower flagship'. This name at once established itself in the language, and America is now called the kwa kee kwoh, the 'flower flag country', and an American, <i>kwa kee kwoh yin</i>, 'flower flag countryman', a more complimentary designation than that of 'red headed barbarian', the name first bestowed upon the Dutch.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Henry_Preble" class="extiw" title="w:George Henry Preble">George H. Preble</a>, as quoted in "Curiosa Sinica" (15 June 1843), by Choong Kwoh, <i>The Boston Courier</i></li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>I gazed on the mountains in grandeur majestic,<br />I gazed on the vales&#8212;they were fruitful and fair;<br />I gazed with delight on the lakes and the fountains,<br />I gazed on the banner&#8212;the eagle was there.<br />"E pluribus unum" exultingly waves,<br />E pluribus unum! what freemen and slaves?<br />The genius of liberty, maiden celestial,<br />Sat nigh that gay banner attempting to smile;<br />Alternately gazing on eagle and fetters,<br />The tears from her eyes trickled down all the while,<br />And she sighed where the banner of liberty waves,<br />o'er traitors, and tyrants, and heart-broken slaves.
<ul><li><i>The Primitive Methodist Magazine</i>, 1862, p. 64 (written 1835)</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>I bow my head to the victims of terrorism. I am highly impressed of the courage of New York residents. The great city and the great American nation are to win!
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://web.archive.org/web/20031117142036/http://www.kremlin.ru/events/photos/2001/11/39974.shtml">inscription at the World Trade Center Memorial Wall</a> (15 November 2001).</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>The U.S. is a very democratic state. There's no doubt about that; and it originally developed as a democratic state. When the first settlers set their foot on the continent, life forced them to forge a relationship and maintain a dialogue with each other to survive. That's why America was conceived as a fundamental democracy.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://web.archive.org/web/20130614041959/http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=33oIF-ggK5U">interview</a> (2013).</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>If <a href="/wiki/Malcolm_X" title="Malcolm X">Malcolm X</a> or the Black Panthers had attempted to set up a separate black state on American soil in the tradition of <a href="/wiki/John_Brown" class="mw-disambig" title="John Brown">John Brown</a>, their efforts would have been crushed immediately. ... A nation which, since its founding, has rejected the idea of hereditary entitlements. Slavery and racial discrimination are exceptions to this tradition. Huge, horrific exceptions, but exceptions nonetheless. For all the hypocrisies and bigotries of its citizens and leaders, the United States does promise liberty, equality and justice. The gap between these promises and realities often yaws wide, but the promises abide. They are part of the 'American Dream', the 'American Creed', and the American 'civil religion', which no amount of 'realism' or cynicism seems able to smother.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jeffrey_J._Pyle" class="extiw" title="w:Jeffrey J. Pyle">Jeff Pyle</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://lawdigitalcommons.bc.edu/cgi/viewcontent.cgi?article=2124&amp;context=bclr">"Race, Equality and the Rule of Law: Critical Race Theory's Attack on the Promises of Liberalism"</a> (May 1999), <i>Boston College Law Review</i></li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li>No group in American history has had more reason to disbelieve America's promises than African Americans... Imbued with Christianity and the American Creed, most black Americans rejected the appeals of socialists in the late nineteenth century, Communists in the 1930s, and neo-Marxist 'liberationists' in the 1960s. Rather, when America's unpaid 'promissory note' came due in the 1950s and 1960s, they marched forth from Christian churches to demand fulfillment of the very American promise that 'all men are created equal'. And faith in the redeemability of America's promises remains in the African-American community today, sustaining efforts to overcome continued segregation, unjust incarceration and enduring economic inequality.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jeffrey_J._Pyle" class="extiw" title="w:Jeffrey J. Pyle">Jeff Pyle</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://lawdigitalcommons.bc.edu/cgi/viewcontent.cgi?article=2124&amp;context=bclr">"Race, Equality and the Rule of Law: Critical Race Theory's Attack on the Promises of Liberalism"</a> (May 1999), <i>Boston College Law Review</i></li></ul></li></ul>

Not in spite of but because of our <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/polyglot" class="extiw" title="wiktionary:polyglot">polyglot</a> background, we have had all the <a href="/wiki/Strength" title="Strength">strength</a> in the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a>. That is the <a href="/wiki/American_way" class="mw-redirect" title="American way">American way</a>. ~ <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Reagan" title="Ronald Reagan">Ronald Reagan</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:USS_Theodore_Roosevelt_(CVN_71)_2015_Deployment_150331-N-GN619-031.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/USS_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28CVN_71%29_2015_Deployment_150331-N-GN619-031.jpg/220px-USS_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28CVN_71%29_2015_Deployment_150331-N-GN619-031.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/USS_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28CVN_71%29_2015_Deployment_150331-N-GN619-031.jpg/330px-USS_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28CVN_71%29_2015_Deployment_150331-N-GN619-031.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/USS_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28CVN_71%29_2015_Deployment_150331-N-GN619-031.jpg/440px-USS_Theodore_Roosevelt_%28CVN_71%29_2015_Deployment_150331-N-GN619-031.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3965" data-file-height="2832" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:USS_Theodore_Roosevelt_(CVN_71)_2015_Deployment_150331-N-GN619-031.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The United States is based on a simple premise. The United States does not start fights. We will never be an aggressor. We maintain our strength in order to deter and defend against aggression; to preserve freedom and peace. ~ <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Reagan" title="Ronald Reagan">Ronald Reagan</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Civil_rights_march_on_washington_dc_schools.tif" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Civil_rights_march_on_washington_dc_schools.tif/lossy-page1-220px-Civil_rights_march_on_washington_dc_schools.tif.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="151" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Civil_rights_march_on_washington_dc_schools.tif/lossy-page1-330px-Civil_rights_march_on_washington_dc_schools.tif.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Civil_rights_march_on_washington_dc_schools.tif/lossy-page1-440px-Civil_rights_march_on_washington_dc_schools.tif.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2819" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Civil_rights_march_on_washington_dc_schools.tif" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">This nation</a> was created to give expression, validity and purpose to our spiritual heritage—the supreme worth of the individual. In such a nation—a nation dedicated to the proposition that <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/All_men_are_created_equal" class="extiw" title="w:All men are created equal">all men are created equal</a>—racial discrimination has no place. ~ <i>Republican Party Platform of 1960</i></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bundesarchiv_Bild_102-09844,_Mussolini_in_Mailand.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Bundesarchiv_Bild_102-09844%2C_Mussolini_in_Mailand.jpg/220px-Bundesarchiv_Bild_102-09844%2C_Mussolini_in_Mailand.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="156" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Bundesarchiv_Bild_102-09844%2C_Mussolini_in_Mailand.jpg/330px-Bundesarchiv_Bild_102-09844%2C_Mussolini_in_Mailand.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Bundesarchiv_Bild_102-09844%2C_Mussolini_in_Mailand.jpg/440px-Bundesarchiv_Bild_102-09844%2C_Mussolini_in_Mailand.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="568" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bundesarchiv_Bild_102-09844,_Mussolini_in_Mailand.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Strangely, it is always America that is described as degenerate and 'fascist', while it is solely in Europe that actual dictatorships and totalitarian regimes spring up. ~ <a href="/wiki/Jean-Fran%C3%A7ois_Revel" title="Jean-François Revel">Jean-Francois Revel</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Constitution_Day_Naturalization_Ceremony_(7996948236).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Constitution_Day_Naturalization_Ceremony_%287996948236%29.jpg/220px-Constitution_Day_Naturalization_Ceremony_%287996948236%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="122" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Constitution_Day_Naturalization_Ceremony_%287996948236%29.jpg/330px-Constitution_Day_Naturalization_Ceremony_%287996948236%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Constitution_Day_Naturalization_Ceremony_%287996948236%29.jpg/440px-Constitution_Day_Naturalization_Ceremony_%287996948236%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4775" data-file-height="2656" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Constitution_Day_Naturalization_Ceremony_(7996948236).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>We are a nation of many nationalities, many races, many religions, bound together by a single unity, the unity of freedom and equality. Whoever seeks to set one nationality against another, seeks to degrade all nationalities. Whoever seeks to set one race against another seeks to enslave all races. Whoever seeks to set one religion against another, seeks to destroy all religion. ~ <a href="/wiki/Franklin_D._Roosevelt" title="Franklin D. Roosevelt">Franklin D. Roosevelt</a></div></div></div>

Any man who says he is an American, but something else also, isn't an American at all. We have room for but one flag, the American flag. ~ <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt" title="Theodore Roosevelt">Theodore Roosevelt</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:DuskDetroit.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/DuskDetroit.jpg/220px-DuskDetroit.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/DuskDetroit.jpg/330px-DuskDetroit.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/DuskDetroit.jpg/440px-DuskDetroit.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="768" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:DuskDetroit.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The immigrant who comes here in good faith becomes an American and assimilates himself to us, he shall be treated on an exact equality with everyone else, for it is an outrage to discriminate against any such man because of creed, or birthplace, or origin. But this is predicated upon the man's becoming in very fact an American, and nothing but an American. If he tries to keep segregated with men of his own origin and separated from the rest of America, then he isn't doing his part as an American. ~ <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt" title="Theodore Roosevelt">Theodore Roosevelt</a></div></div></div>
